NOTICE

MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

3439

PUBLIC NOTICE
FORM No. 155
(See Rule 329)
Members Voluntary Winding up
SLEEVES INDIA AUTOMOTIVE PRIVATE LIMITED
Notice convening Final Meeting

Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 of the Companies Act, 1956 that a General Meeting of the members
of the above named Company will be held at the Registered Office at No. 12A, Kuppusamy Road, Poothapedu, Ramapuram,
Chennai-600 089 on the 20th day of December 2014, at 4.00 p.m. for the purpose of having an account laid before them
showing the manner in which the winding up has been conducted and the property of the Company disposed of and of
hearing any explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a Special Resolution of the Company,
the manner in which the books, accounts and documents of the Company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.

Chennai,
13th November 2014.

V.B.R. MENON,
Liquidator.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
